Technical notes regarding the database text

Text was taken from Quran for Android.
(by Quran.com, which in turn most likely took it from the ebook on Shamela.org, which is the 1st edition by Resalah Publishers. This seems to be the only electronic text of of this book out there.)
Directory: Files, / data / data / com.quran.labs.androidquran / files / quran_android / databases / quran.ar.sa3dy.db
table: verses, column: text
Extracted the database on 18/2/24.
It had rows with just a number, even multiple such rows, which were supposed to be repeated I think, as the tafsir wasnt exactly on a per ayah basis, as it sometimes covered multiple ayahs in the same block of tafsir. So I replaced those numbers to be blank, then replaced the empty row or rows with the next closest row with text.
with:
